# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# OpenJDK G1 GC Garbage Collection Cycle Chain

## Your Task

Trace the G1 garbage collector's concurrent marking and mixed collection cycle in openjdk/jdk. Find C++ source files implementing: the G1ConcurrentMark start trigger, the SATB marking queue processing, the remembered set scanning, and the mixed collection region selection.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/jdk--742e735d.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/jdk--742e735d` (openjdk/jdk)

```json

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

67-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully traced the G1 garbage collector's concurrent marking and mixed collection cycle in openjdk/jdk. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Components Identified:

**G1ConcurrentMark Start Trigger:**
- `G1IHOPControl` - Determines when to initiate concurrent marking based on old generation allocation threshold
- `G1CollectorState` - Tracks collection states including `in_concurrent_start_gc()` flag
- `G1ConcurrentMarkThread` - Orchestrates the complete marking cycle

**SATB Marking Queue Processing:**
- `G1SATBMarkQueueSet` - Manages G1-specific SATB queue sets
- `SATBMarkQueue` - Core queue abstraction for buffering marked references
- `G1ThreadLocalData` - Thread-local storage for SATB queues

**Remembered Set Scanning:**
- `G1RemSet` - Main remembered set interface with scanning capabilities
- `G1RemSetScanState` - Manages scan state and card table scanning
- `G1HeapRegionRemSet` - Per-region remembered set tracking cross-region references
- `G1ConcurrentRebuildAndScrub` - Rebuilds remembered sets after marking

**Mixed Collection Region Selection:**
- `G1CollectionSetChooser` - Sorts candidate regions by GC efficiency
- `G1CollectionSetCandidates` - Stores and manages selected old regions
- `G1YoungCollector` - Executes evacuation of young and selected old regions

**Key Marking Operations:**
- `G1CMTask` - Executes concurrent marking work
- `G1CMOopClosure` - Iterates over object references during marking

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file paths, symbols, and a detailed narrative explaining the cycle chain.

implements the Implicit Hoist Ordering Policy to determine when old generation allocation has reached a threshold requiring mark cycle initiation. The G1CollectorState (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectorState.hpp/cpp) tracks the collection state, particularly the in_concurrent_start_gc() flag which indicates when a concurrent start GC is in progress.\\n\\n**Concurrent Mark Cycle Orchestration:**\\nThe G1ConcurrentMarkThread (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMarkThread.hpp/cpp) manages the overall marking cycle phases. It calls concurrent_cycle_start() in G1ConcurrentMark (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.hpp/cpp), then progresses through multiple phases: phase_scan_root_regions(), phase_mark_loop() with subphases including mark_from_roots() and preclean(), followed by phase_rebuild_and_scrub() and phase_cleanup().\\n\\n**SATB Marking Queue Processing:**\\nDuring concurrent marking, the Snapshot-At-The-Beginning (SATB) marking queue system ensures correctness. G1SATBMarkQueueSet (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1SATBMarkQueueSet.hpp/cpp) manages thread-local SATB queues (inherited from SATBMarkQueue in src/hotspot/share/gc/shared/satbMarkQueue.hpp/cpp). Each thread's SATB queue is accessed via G1ThreadLocalData (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ThreadLocalData.hpp), which stores references to objects written during marking.\\n\\n**Marking Task Execution:**\\nThe G1CMTask class (defined in src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentMark.hpp/cpp) executes the actual marking work. It uses G1CMOopClosure (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1OopClosures.hpp/cpp) to iterate over object references and mark live objects. Tasks are queued in task queues (G1CMTaskQueue/G1CMTaskQueueSet) and executed by multiple worker threads.\\n\\n**Remembered Set Scanning and Rebuild:**\\nAfter marking completes, the G1ConcurrentRebuildAndScrub (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentRebuildAndScrub.hpp/cpp) class handles rebuilding and scrubbing remembered sets. The G1RemSet (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSet.hpp/cpp) manages the remembered set infrastructure with G1RemSetScanState for scan state tracking. Each G1HeapRegion has a G1HeapRegionRemSet (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1HeapRegionRemSet.hpp/cpp) that tracks cross-region references using card tables.\\n\\n**Mixed Collection Region Selection:**\\nAfter marking completes and remark is finished, the G1CollectionSetChooser (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetChooser.hpp/cpp) builds a sorted list of candidate regions for mixed collection. The static build() method processes all regions and calculates GC efficiency metrics. Candidate regions are stored in G1CollectionSetCandidates (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetCandidates.hpp/cpp). The G1YoungCollector (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1YoungCollector.hpp/cpp) then performs evacuation of young and selected old regions during mixed GC pauses. The G1Policy (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1Policy.hpp/cpp) makes decisions on which regions to include based on evacuation predictions and pause time targets.\\n\\nThe entire cycle is coordinated within G1CollectedHeap (src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectedHeap.hpp/cpp) which orchestrates the do_collection_pause_at_safepoint() operations that transition between young-only and mixed collection phases.\"\n}\n",
